<script type="text/javascript" async=true>
(function() {
  var host = "www.themoneytizer.com";
  var element = document.createElement('script');
  var firstScript = document.getElementsByTagName('script')[0];
  var url = 'https://cmp.inmobi.com'
    .concat('/choice/', '6Fv0cGNfc_bw8', '/', host, '/choice.js?tag_version=V3');
  var uspTries = 0;
  var uspTriesLimit = 3;
  element.async = true;
  element.type = 'text/javascript';
  element.src = url;

  firstScript.parentNode.insertBefore(element, firstScript);

  function makeStub() {
    var TCF_LOCATOR_NAME = '__tcfapiLocator';
    var queue = [];
    var win = window;
    var cmpFrame;

    function addFrame() {
      var doc = win.document;
      var otherCMP = !!(win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]);

      if (!otherCMP) {
        if (doc.body) {
          var iframe = doc.createElement('iframe');

          iframe.style.cssText = 'display:none';
          iframe.name = TCF_LOCATOR_NAME;
          doc.body.appendChild(iframe);
        } else {
          setTimeout(addFrame, 5);
        }
      }
      return !otherCMP;
    }

    function tcfAPIHandler() {
      var gdprApplies;
      var args = arguments;

      if (!args.length) {
        return queue;
      } else if (args[0] === 'setGdprApplies') {
        if (
          args.length > 3 &&
          args[2] === 2 &&
          typeof args[3] === 'boolean'
        ) {
          gdprApplies = args[3];
          if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
            args[2]('set', true);
          }
        }
      } else if (args[0] === 'ping') {
        var retr = {
          gdprApplies: gdprApplies,
          cmpLoaded: false,
          cmpStatus: 'stub'
        };

        if (typeof args[2] === 'function') {
          args[2](retr);
        }
      } else {
        if(args[0] === 'init' && typeof args[3] === 'object') {
          args[3] = Object.assign(args[3], { tag_version: 'V3' });
        }
        queue.push(args);
      }
    }

    function postMessageEventHandler(event) {
      var msgIsString = typeof event.data === 'string';
      var json = {};

      try {
        if (msgIsString) {
          json = JSON.parse(event.data);
        } else {
          json = event.data;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      var payload = json.__tcfapiCall;

      if (payload) {
        window.__tcfapi(
          payload.command,
          payload.version,
          function(retValue, success) {
            var returnMsg = {
              __tcfapiReturn: {
                returnValue: retValue,
                success: success,
                callId: payload.callId
              }
            };
            if (msgIsString) {
              returnMsg = JSON.stringify(returnMsg);
            }
            if (event && event.source && event.source.postMessage) {
              event.source.postMessage(returnMsg, '*');
            }
          },
          payload.parameter
        );
      }
    }

    while (win) {
      try {
        if (win.frames[TCF_LOCATOR_NAME]) {
          cmpFrame = win;
          break;
        }
      } catch (ignore) {}

      if (win === window.top) {
        break;
      }
      win = win.parent;
    }
    if (!cmpFrame) {
      addFrame();
      win.__tcfapi = tcfAPIHandler;
      win.addEventListener('message', postMessageEventHandler, false);
    }
  };

  makeStub();

  var uspStubFunction = function() {
    var arg = arguments;
    if (typeof window.__uspapi !== uspStubFunction) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        if (typeof window.__uspapi !== 'undefined') {
          window.__uspapi.apply(window.__uspapi, arg);
        }
      }, 500);
    }
  };

  var checkIfUspIsReady = function() {
    uspTries++;
    if (window.__uspapi === uspStubFunction && uspTries < uspTriesLimit) {
      console.warn('USP is not accessible');
    } else {
      clearInterval(uspInterval);
    }
  };

  if (typeof window.__uspapi === 'undefined') {
    window.__uspapi = uspStubFunction;
    var uspInterval = setInterval(checkIfUspIsReady, 6000);
  }
})();
</script>

  /* 🌟 Bloc sticky top, caché au départ */
  #stickyAdTop {
    position: fixed;
    top: -100px;                        /* caché au-dessus de l’écran */
    left: 50%;
    transform: translateX(-50%);
    width: 90vw;
    max-width: 600px;
    height: 60px;

    background: #fff;

    z-index: 99999;

    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    padding: 0;
    line-height: 0;

    transition: top 0.35s ease;         /* glissement smooth */
  }

  .adTopRow {
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    width: 100%;
  }

  .adTopContainer {
    flex: 1;
    display: flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
  }

  /* Empêchez la pub de dépasser */
  #stickyAdTop .adsbygoogle {
    width: 100% !important;
    height: 100% !important;
    object-fit: contain !important;
    display: block !important;
  }

  /* 📱 Mobile */
  @media (max-width: 600px) {
    #stickyAdTop {
      width: 95vw;
      max-width: 340px;
      height: 70px;
      top: -120px;
    }
    #stickyAdTop .adsbygoogle {
      height: 70px !important;
    }

<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
  let lastScrollY = window.scrollY;
  const topAd = document.getElementById("stickyAdTop");

  if (!topAd) return;

  window.addEventListener("scroll", function () {

    // 🡳 Descente → afficher
    if (window.scrollY > lastScrollY && window.scrollY > 120) {
      topAd.style.top = "12px";          // slide-down
    }
    // 🡱 Remontée → cacher
    else {
      topAd.style.top = "-120px";        // slide-up
    }

    lastScrollY = window.scrollY;
  });
});
</script>

<!-- Slide image pour NordVPN -->

<script>
(function(){
  const blocks = document.querySelectorAll('.jtr-compare');
  blocks.forEach(block => {
    const wrap = block.querySelector('.jtr-compare__wrap');
    const range = block.querySelector('.jtr-compare__range');
    const start = block.getAttribute('data-start');
    if (start) range.value = start;

    const setPos = (v) => {
      const val = Math.min(100, Math.max(0, Number(v)));
      wrap.style.setProperty('--pos', val + '%');
    };
    setPos(range.value);

    range.addEventListener('input', (e) => setPos(e.target.value));

    // Drag “à la souris/tactile”
    let down = false;
    const onMove = (clientX) => {
      const r = wrap.getBoundingClientRect();
      const pct = ((clientX - r.left) / r.width) * 100;
      range.value = pct;
      setPos(pct);
    };

    wrap.addEventListener('pointerdown', (e) => { down = true; wrap.setPointerCapture(e.pointerId); onMove(e.clientX); });
    wrap.addEventListener('pointermove', (e) => { if (down) onMove(e.clientX); });
    wrap.addEventListener('pointerup', () => { down = false; });
    wrap.addEventListener('pointercancel', () => { down = false; });
  });
})();
</script>



<!-- Script FAQ SMOOTH (VPN + OA) -->
<script>
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {

  function setupSmoothFAQ(detailsSelector, contentSelector){
    const faqs = document.querySelectorAll(detailsSelector);

    faqs.forEach(details => {
      const summary = details.querySelector('summary');
      const content = details.querySelector(contentSelector);
      if (!summary || !content) return;

      // État initial (si open est présent dans le HTML)
      if (details.hasAttribute('open')) {
        details.classList.add('is-open');
        content.style.height = content.scrollHeight + 'px';
        requestAnimationFrame(() => { content.style.height = 'auto'; });
      }

      let animating = false;

      const openFAQ = () => {
        if (animating) return;
        animating = true;

        details.open = true;
        details.classList.add('is-open');

        content.style.height = '0px';
        content.offsetHeight; // reflow

        const target = content.scrollHeight;
        content.style.height = target + 'px';

        const onEnd = (e) => {
          if (e.propertyName !== 'height') return;
          content.style.height = 'auto';
          content.removeEventListener('transitionend', onEnd);
          animating = false;
        };
        content.addEventListener('transitionend', onEnd);
      };

      const closeFAQ = () => {
        if (animating) return;
        animating = true;

        const start = content.scrollHeight;
        content.style.height = start + 'px';
        content.offsetHeight; // reflow

        details.classList.remove('is-open');
        content.style.height = '0px';

        const onEnd = (e) => {
          if (e.propertyName !== 'height') return;
          details.open = false;
          content.removeEventListener('transitionend', onEnd);
          animating = false;
        };
        content.addEventListener('transitionend', onEnd);
      };

      summary.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault(); // on garde ton choix : pas de toggle natif
        if (details.open) closeFAQ();
        else openFAQ();
      });
    });
  }

  // ✅ VPN FAQ
  setupSmoothFAQ('details.vpn-faq', '.a');

  // ✅ Contact / Privacy FAQ
  setupSmoothFAQ('details.oa-faq', '.oa-faq__a');

});
</script>

              if (obj.addEventListener)

          function highlight_adblocked_ads() {
              try {
                  var ad_wrappers = document.querySelectorAll('div[id^="quads-ad"]')
              } catch (e) {
                  return;
              }
              for (i = 0; i < ad_wrappers.length; i++) {
                  ad_wrappers[i].className += ' quads-highlight-adblocked';
                  ad_wrappers[i].setAttribute('style', 'display:block !important');
              }
          }

          addEvent1(w, 'load', function () {
              if (wpquads_adblocker_check === undefined || wpquads_adblocker_check === false) {
                  highlight_adblocked_ads();
              }
          });

      })(document, window);
   </script>
   	</body>
</html>
